warp $at 0x0 0x0 	// int handler start
add $k0 $0 $0
addi $k0 1 			// west button , does not work when two or more interrupts are hit before handling.
bne $at $k0 1
j 0x01a
add $k0 $k0 $k0  	// south button
bne $at $k0 0x1
j 0x01b
add $k0 $k0 $k0 	// east button
bne $at $k0 0x1
j 0x01c
add $k0 $k0 $k0 	// north button
bne $at $k0 0x1 
j 0x01d
add $k0 $k0 $k0		// sw0
bne $at $k0 0x1 
j 0x025 			// run euclid
add $k0 $k0 $k0 	// sw1
bne $at $k0 0x1
j 0x01e
add $k0 $k0 $k0 	// sw2
bne $at $k0 0x1
j 0x021
add $k0 $k0 $k0 	// sw3
bne $at $k0 0x1
j 0x024
warp $0 0x0 0x1 	// west clear
warp $0 0x1 0x1 	// south clear
warp $0 0x2 0x1 	// east clear
warp $0 0x3 0x1 	// north clear
warp $0 0x1 0x2 	// sw1 read
add $0 $0 $0
warp $0 0x5 0x1 	// sw1 clear
warp $0 0x0 0x2 	// sw2 read
add $0 $0 $0
warp $0 0x6 0x1 	// sw2 clear
warp $0 0x7 0x1 	// sw3 clear
add $sp $0 $0 		// euclid start sw0 goes here
lui $sp 0x00
ori $sp 0xff
lui $a0 0x2f 		// added 3 lines...loads $a0.
ori $a0 0xf0
lw $a0 $a0 0
add $a1 $0 $0
addi $a1 2
add $t0 $0 $0
add $t1 $0 $0
add $t2 $0 $0
add $t3 $0 $0
add $s0 $0 $0
add $s1 $0 $0
add $s2 $0 $0
add $ra $0 $0
lui $ra 0x30
ori $ra 0x59
add $rv $0 $0
add $at $0 $0
add $k0 $0 $0
add $k1 $0 $0
addi $sp -3
sw $ra $sp 0
sw $a0 $sp 2
lw $a0 $sp 2
sw $a1 $sp 1
jal 0x04a
lw $a1 $sp 1
addi $a1 1
addi $rv -1
bne $rv $0 0x9
add $rv $0 $a1
addi $rv -1
lw $ra $sp 0
addi $sp 3
jr $ra
bne $a0 $0 0x1 		// gcd
j 0x055 			// 12382, jumps to [1]
bne $a1 $0 0x1 		// while loop
j 0x057 			// 12384, jumps to [2]
beq $a1 $a0 0x4
slt $t0 $a1 $a0
beq $t0 $0 0x2
sub $a0 $a0 $a1
j 0x04c
sub $a1 $a1 $a0
j 0x04c
add $rv $a1 $0 		// [1]
jr $ra
add $rv $a0 $0 		// [2]
jr $ra
lui $t0 0x2f
ori $t0 0xf2
sw $rv $t0 0
warp $0 0x2 0x3 	// Display
add $0 $0 $0
warp $0 0x4 0x1 	// Clear
